  284. Finally, a TRUE back shaver! The size of this shaver makes it easy for even the least agile person to reach every area of the back. The push button to lock the angle is hardly necessary and you could damage the ratcheting joint if you try to adjust the angle without unlocking it first. This shaver will not operate while the charger is plugged in (an annoying feature of all shavers of this type) but most people should be able to complete their shave long before the battery runs low.
